<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Fieldset</code> component provides contexts such as <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">invalid</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">disabled</code> for form elements. While most Ark UI
components natively support these contexts, you can also use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> component with standard HTML form elements.</p>
<h3 id="basic" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#basic"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Basic</h3>

<h3 id="field" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#field"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Field</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">This example demonstrates how to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field</code> component with a standard input field within a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Fieldset</code>.</p>

<h3 id="checkbox" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#checkbox"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Checkbox</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">This example shows how to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Fieldset</code> component with other Ark UI form elements like <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Checkbox</code>.</p>

<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the fieldset is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useFieldset</code> hook. This way
you can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_4vhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_4vhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_4vhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="input-with-select" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#input-with-select"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Input with Select</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">This example shows how to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Fieldset</code> component with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Field.Input</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Select</code> to create a interactive phone
input component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_55hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_55hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_55hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>

Anatomy\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"fieldset\" /\u003e\n\n```tsx\n\u003cFieldset.Root\u003e\n  \u003cFieldset.Legend /\u003e\n  \u003cFieldset.HelperText /\u003e\n  \u003cFieldset.ErrorText /\u003e\n\u003c/Fieldset.Root\u003e\n```\n\n## Examples\n\nThe `Fieldset` component provides contexts such as `invalid` and `disabled` for form elements. While most Ark UI\ncomponents natively support these contexts, you can also use the `Field` component with standard HTML form elements.\n\n### Basic\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### '@ark-ui/svelte/fieldset'\n  import field from 'styles/field.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/fieldset.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cFieldset.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n  \u003cFieldset.Legend class={styles.Legend}\u003eContact Details\u003c/Fieldset.Legend\u003e\n\n  \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cField.Label class={field.Label}\u003eName\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n    \u003cField.Input class={field.Input} placeholder=\"John Doe\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n  \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cField.Label class={field.Label}\u003eEmail\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n    \u003cField.Input class={field.Input} type=\"email\" placeholder=\"john@example.com\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\u003c/Fieldset.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Field\n\nThis example demonstrates how to use the `Field` component with a standard input field within a `Fieldset`.\n\n**Example: with-field**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { Fieldset } from '@ark-ui/react/fieldset'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/fieldset.module.css'\n\nexport const WithField = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cFieldset.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cFieldset.Legend className={styles.Legend}\u003ePersonal Information\u003c/Fieldset.Legend\u003e\n\n      \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cField.Label className={field.Label}\u003eFirst Name\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n        \u003cField.Input className={field.Input} placeholder=\"Enter your first name\" /\u003e\n        \u003cField.HelperText className={field.HelperText}\u003eAs it appears on your ID\u003c/Field.HelperText\u003e\n      \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n      \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cField.Label with-checkbox**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Checkbox } from '@ark-ui/react/checkbox'\nimport { Fieldset } from '@ark-ui/react/fieldset'\nimport { CheckIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport checkbox \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n        \u003c/Checkbox.Control\u003e\n        \u003cCheckbox.Label className={checkbox.Label}\u003eProduct updates\u003c/Checkbox.Label\u003e\n \u003cCheckbox.Control class={checkbox.Control}\u003e\n      \u003cCheckbox.Indicator class={checkbox.Indicator}\u003e\n        \u003cCheckIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/Checkbox.Indicator\u003e\n \u003c/Checkbox.Root\u003e\n\u003c/Fieldset.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the fieldset is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useFieldset` hook. This way\nyou can access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { Fieldset, useFieldset } from '@ark-ui/react/fieldset'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/fieldset.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const fieldset = useFieldset()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFieldset.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={fieldset}\u003e\n      \u003cFieldset.Legend className={styles.Legend}\u003eContact Details\u003c/Fieldset.Legend\u003e\n\n      \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cField.Label className={field.Label}\u003eName\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n        \u003cField.Input className={field.Input} placeholder=\"John Doe\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n      \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cField.Label className={field.Label}\u003eEmail\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n        \u003cField.Input className={field.Input} type=\"email\" placeholder=\"john@example.com\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/Fieldset.RootProvider\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/solid/field'\nimport { Fieldset, useFieldset } from '@ark-ui/solid/fieldset'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/fieldset.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const fieldset = useFieldset()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFieldset.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={fieldset}\u003e\n      \u003cFieldset.Legend class={styles.Legend}\u003eContact Details\u003c/Fieldset.Legend\u003e\n\n      \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cField.Label class={field.Label}\u003eName\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n        \u003cField.Input class={field.Input} placeholder=\"John Doe\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n      \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n        \u003cField.Label class={field.Label}\u003eEmail\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n        \u003cField.Input class={field.Input} type=\"email\" placeholder=\"john@example.com\" /\u003e\n      \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/Fieldset.RootProvider\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/vue/field'\nimport { Fieldset, useFieldset } from '@ark-ui/vue/fieldset'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/fieldset.module.css'\n\nconst fieldset = useFieldset()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cFieldset.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"fieldset\"\u003e\n    \u003cFieldset.Legend :class=\"styles.Legend\"\u003eContact Details\u003c/Fieldset.Legend\u003e\n\n    \u003cField.Root :class=\"field.Root\"\u003e\n      \u003cField.Label :class=\"field.Label\"\u003eName\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n      \u003cField.Input :class=\"field.Input\" placeholder=\"John Doe\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n    \u003cField.Root :class=\"field.Root\"\u003e\n      \u003cField.Label :class=\"field.Label\"\u003eEmail\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n      \u003cField.Input :class=\"field.Input\" type=\"email\" placeholder=\"john@example.com\" /\u003e\n    \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n  \u003c/Fieldset.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Field } from '@ark-ui/svelte/field'\n  import { Fieldset, useFieldset } from '@ark-ui/svelte/fieldset'\n  import field from 'styles/field.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/fieldset.module.css'\n\n  const fieldset = useFieldset()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cFieldset.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={fieldset}\u003e\n  \u003cFieldset.Legend class={styles.Legend}\u003eContact Details\u003c/Fieldset.Legend\u003e\n\n  \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cField.Label class={field.Label}\u003eName\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n    \u003cField.Input class={field.Input} placeholder=\"John Doe\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n  \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n    \u003cField.Label class={field.Label}\u003eEmail\u003c/Field.Label\u003e\n    \u003cField.Input class={field.Input} type=\"email\" placeholder=\"john@example.com\" /\u003e\n  \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\u003c/Fieldset.RootProvider\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Input with Select\n\nThis example shows how to use the `Fieldset` component with `Field.Input` and `Select` to create a interactive phone\ninput component.\n\n**Example: phone-input**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/react/field'\nimport { Fieldset } from '@ark-ui/react/fieldset'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { Select, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/react/select'\nimport { ChevronsUpDownIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useRef } from 'react'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/fieldset.module.css'\nimport select from 'styles/select.module.css'\n\nexport const PhoneInput = () =\u003e {\n  const extensions = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: '+1', value: '+1' },\n      { label: '+44', value: '+44' },\n      { label: '+49', value: '+49' },\n      { label: '+41', value: '+41' },\n    ],\n  })\n\n  const inputRef = useRef\u003cHTMLInputElement | null\u003e(null)\n  const focusInput = () =\u003e {\n    setTimeout(() =\u003e {\n      inputRef.current?.focus()\n    })\n  }\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFieldset.Root className={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cFieldset.Legend className={styles.Legend} onClick={focusInput}\u003e\n        Mobile Number\n      \u003c/Fieldset.Legend\u003e\n\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'flex-start', gap: '0.5rem' }}\u003e\n        \u003cField.Root\u003e\n          \u003cSelect.Root className={select.Root} collection={extensions} defaultValue={['+1']} onValueChange={focusInput}\u003e\n            \u003cSelect.Control className={select.Control}\u003e\n              \u003cSelect.Trigger className={select.Trigger}\u003e\n                \u003cSelect.ValueText placeholder=\"Select\" /\u003e\n                \u003cChevronsUpDownIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Select.Trigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Select.Control\u003e\n            \u003cPortal\u003e\n              \u003cSelect.Positioner\u003e\n                \u003cSelect.Content className={select.Content}\u003e\n                  {extensions.items.map((item) =\u003e (\n                    \u003cSelect.Item className={select.Item} key={item.value} item={item}\u003e\n                      \u003cSelect.ItemText className={select.ItemText}\u003e{item.label}\u003c/Select.ItemText\u003e\n                    \u003c/Select.Item\u003e\n                  ))}\n                \u003c/Select.Content\u003e\n              \u003c/Select.Positioner\u003e\n            \u003c/Portal\u003e\n            \u003cSelect.HiddenSelect /\u003e\n          \u003c/Select.Root\u003e\n        \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n        \u003cField.Root className={field.Root}\u003e\n          \u003cField.Input className={field.Input} ref={inputRef} /\u003e\n        \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n      \u003c/div\u003e\n    \u003c/Fieldset.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Field } from '@ark-ui/solid/field'\nimport { Fieldset } from '@ark-ui/solid/fieldset'\nimport { Select, createListCollection } from '@ark-ui/solid/select'\nimport { ChevronsUpDownIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Index, createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/fieldset.module.css'\nimport select from 'styles/select.module.css'\n\nexport const PhoneInput = () =\u003e {\n  const extensions = createListCollection({\n    items: [\n      { label: '+1', value: '+1' },\n      { label: '+44', value: '+44' },\n      { label: '+49', value: '+49' },\n      { label: '+41', value: '+41' },\n    ],\n  })\n\n  const [inputRef, setInputRef] = createSignal\u003cHTMLInputElement | null\u003e(null)\n\n  const focusInput = () =\u003e {\n    setTimeout(() =\u003e {\n      inputRef()?.focus()\n    })\n  }\n\n  return (\n    \u003cFieldset.Root class={styles.Root}\u003e\n      \u003cFieldset.Legend class={styles.Legend} onClick={focusInput}\u003e\n        Mobile Number\n      \u003c/Fieldset.Legend\u003e\n\n      \u003cdiv style={{ display: 'flex', 'align-items': 'flex-start', gap: '0.5rem' }}\u003e\n        \u003cField.Root\u003e\n          \u003cSelect.Root class={select.Root} collection={extensions} defaultValue={['+1']} onValueChange={focusInput}\u003e\n            \u003cSelect.Control class={select.Control}\u003e\n              \u003cSelect.Trigger class={select.Trigger}\u003e\n                \u003cSelect.ValueText placeholder=\"Select\" /\u003e\n                \u003cChevronsUpDownIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Select.Trigger\u003e\n            \u003c/Select.Control\u003e\n            \u003cPortal\u003e\n              \u003cSelect.Positioner\u003e\n                \u003cSelect.Content class={select.Content}\u003e\n                  \u003cIndex each={extensions.items}\u003e\n                    {(item) =\u003e (\n                      \u003cSelect.Item class={select.Item} item={item()}\u003e\n                        \u003cSelect.ItemText class={select.ItemText}\u003e{item().label}\u003c/Select.ItemText\u003e\n                      \u003c/Select.Item\u003e\n                    )}\n                  \u003c/Index\u003e\n                \u003c/Select.Content\u003e\n              \u003c/Select.Positioner\u003e\n            \u003c/Portal\u003e\n            \u003cSelect.HiddenSelect /\u003e\n          \u003c/Select.Root\u003e\n        \u003c/Field.Root\u003e\n\n        \u003cField.Root class={field.Root}\u003e\n          \u003cField.Input class={field.Input} ref={setInputRef} /\u003e\n
